  <script>

    window.docCookies = {
      getItem: function (sKey) {
        if (!sKey) { return null; }
        return decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;)\\s*" + encodeURIComponent(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\\$&") + "\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$"), "$1")) || null;
      },
      setItem: function (sKey, sValue, vEnd, sPath, sDomain, bSecure) {
        if (!sKey || /^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(sKey)) { return false; }
        var sExpires = "";
        if (vEnd) {
          switch (vEnd.constructor) {
            case Number:
              sExpires = vEnd === Infinity ? "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT" : "; max-age=" + vEnd;
              break;
            case String:
              sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd;
              break;
            case Date:
              sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd.toUTCString();
              break;
          }
        }
        document.cookie = encodeURIComponent(sKey) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(sValue) + sExpires + (sDomain ? "; domain=" + sDomain : "") + (sPath ? "; path=" + sPath : "") + (bSecure ? "; secure" : "");
        return true;
      },
      removeItem: function (sKey, sPath, sDomain) {
        if (!this.hasItem(sKey)) { return false; }
        document.cookie = encodeURIComponent(sKey) + "=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT" + (sDomain ? "; domain=" + sDomain : "") + (sPath ? "; path=" + sPath : "");
        return true;
      },
      hasItem: function (sKey) {
        if (!sKey) { return false; }
        return (new RegExp("(?:^|;\\s*)" + encodeURIComponent(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\\$&") + "\\s*\\=")).test(document.cookie);
      },
      keys: function () {
        var aKeys = document.cookie.replace(/((?:^|\s*;)[^\=]+)(?=;|$)|^\s*|\s*(?:\=[^;]*)?(?:\1|$)/g, "").split(/\s*(?:\=[^;]*)?;\s*/);
        for (var nLen = aKeys.length, nIdx = 0; nIdx < nLen; nIdx++) { aKeys[nIdx] = decodeURIComponent(aKeys[nIdx]); }
        return aKeys;
      }
    };

    window.identify = function() {
        analytics.identify();
    }
  </script>

   <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
    $(document).ready(function(){
      // Hide Header on on scroll down
      var didScroll;
      var lastScrollTop = 0;
      var delta = 5;
      var headerHeight = $('header').outerHeight();
  
      $(window).scroll(function(event){
        didScroll = true;
      });
  
      setInterval(function() {
        if (didScroll) {
          hasScrolled();
          didScroll = false;
        }
      }, 250);
  
      function hasScrolled() {
        var st = $(this).scrollTop();
    
        // Make sure they scroll more than delta
        if(Math.abs(lastScrollTop - st) <= delta)
          return;
    
        // If they scrolled down and are past the navbar, add class .nav-up.
        // This is necessary so you never see what is "behind" the navbar.
        if (st > lastScrollTop && st > headerHeight){
          // Scroll Down
          $('.navigation__header').removeClass('header-down').addClass('header-up');
        } else {
          // Scroll Up
          if(st + $(window).height() < $(document).height()) {
            $('.navigation__header').removeClass('header-up').addClass('header-down');
          }
        }
    
        lastScrollTop = st;
      }
    });

    // Collapsable Search Field
    $('.search-field__holder.collapsed').on('click', function(e) {
      $(this).removeClass('collapsed').addClass('expanded').find('.search-field__input').focus();
    });

    $(document).on('touchstart', function() {
      documentClick = true;
    });
    $(document).on('touchmove', function() {
      documentClick = false;
    });

    $(document).on('click touchend', function (event) {
      if (event.type == 'click') documentClick = true;
      if (documentClick){
        if(!$(event.target).closest('.navigation__header .search-field__holder').length) {
          if($('.navigation__header .search-field__holder').hasClass('expanded')) {
            $('.navigation__header .search-field__holder').addClass('collapsed').removeClass('expanded');
          }
        }
      }
    })
  </script>

         <table class="table table-condensed"> 
          <tbody>
           <tr id="lesson-row-2150" class="lesson-row "> 
            <td class="cell cell-pseudo-checkbox"> <span class="pseudo-checkbox-holder"> <i id="completed-icon-2150-true" class="pseudo-checkbox" style="display: none"></i> <i id="uncompleted-icon-2150-true" class="pseudo-checkbox" style="display: none"></i> </span> <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
                $(function() {
                  var completed = $('#completed-icon-2150-true'),
                      uncompleted = $('#uncompleted-icon-2150-true'),
                      tile = $('#lesson-tile-2150'),
                      row = $('#lesson-row-2150');

                  $("#lesson-row-2150 td").on("click", function(e) {
                    if( $(this).hasClass('cell-add-to') ) return;
                    if (e.isDefaultPrevented() || e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey || e.which === 2) {
                      return;
                    }
                    document.location = "https://egghead.io/lessons/javascript-handle-errors-in-asynchronous-functions";
                  });

                  completed.hide();
                  uncompleted.show();

                  completed.click(function(event) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                    completed.hide();
                    uncompleted.show();
                    row.removeClass('lesson-watched');
                    tile.removeClass('lesson-watched');
                    $.ajax({
                      type: "POST",
                      url: '/watch/manual_uncomplete',
                      data: {
                        lesson_view: {
                          lesson_id: 2150
                        }
                      },
                      dataType: "json"
                    })
                  });

            <h4 class="title"> <span class="pseudo-checkbox-holder"> <i id="completed-icon-1891-false" class="pseudo-checkbox" style="display: none"></i> <i id="uncompleted-icon-1891-false" class="pseudo-checkbox" style="display: none"></i> </span> Publish npm packages using npm publish </h4> 
            <div class="info-line"> 
             <small class="duration"><i class="icon-time"></i> 1:29</small> 
             <small class="folder"><i class="icon-folder-open-alt"></i> js</small> 
            </div> 
            <!-- info-line --> 
            <small class="description"><p>In this lesson we will publish our package. We will first add a <code>prepublish</code> script that runs our <code>build</code> script; this will ensure the built folder gets added to npm when published. We will also add a <code>.npmignore</code> so that only our built files get installed. We need to run <code>npm adduser</code> to log in to an npm account. We can then run <code>npm publish</code> to publish our package and view it on npm.</p> <p>Note: if you want to actually publish the package from this course, you'll need to rename it since <code>sensitive-words</code> is already taken. You can use a <a href="https://docs.npmjs.com/misc/scope">scoped package name</a> for this as well.</p> </small> 
           </div>

         <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
  $(function() {
    var completed = $('#completed-icon-1891-false'),
        uncompleted = $('#uncompleted-icon-1891-false'),
        tile = $('#lesson-tile-1891'),
        row = $('#lesson-row-1891');



    completed.hide();
    uncompleted.show();

    completed.click(function() {
      completed.hide();
      uncompleted.show();
      row.removeClass('lesson-watched');
      tile.removeClass('lesson-watched');
      $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: '/watch/manual_uncomplete',
        data: {
          lesson_view: {
            lesson_id: 1891
          }
        },
        dataType: "json"
      })
    });

    uncompleted.click(function() {
      completed.show();
      uncompleted.hide();
      row.addClass('lesson-watched');
      tile.addClass('lesson-watched');
      $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: '/watch/manual_complete',
        data: {
          lesson_view: {
            lesson_id: 1891
          }
        },
        dataType: "json"
      })
    });

  });
</script>

            <h4 class="title"> <span class="pseudo-checkbox-holder"> <i id="completed-icon-1854-false" class="pseudo-checkbox" style="display: none"></i> <i id="uncompleted-icon-1854-false" class="pseudo-checkbox" style="display: none"></i> </span> Test npm packages locally in another project using npm link </h4> 
            <div class="info-line"> 
             <small class="duration"><i class="icon-time"></i> 4:01</small> 
             <small class="folder"><i class="icon-folder-open-alt"></i> js</small> 
            </div> 
            <!-- info-line --> 
            <small class="description"><p>We will import our newly published package into a new project locally to make sure everything is working as expected. We can do this locally before publishing with <code>npm link</code>. This creates a symbolic link in our <code>node_modules</code> folder, so our unpublished local package is used like an installed published package. This is important because it lets us test making changes to our package and using them immediately without publishing and updating a package with each change we want to test. This is good practice to do before publishing a new version of a package.</p> </small> 
           </div>
